cuda_source = r'''
#include <torch/extension.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <math.h>

__global__ void msa_proj_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ x,
    float* __restrict__ q, float* __restrict__ k, float* __restrict__ v, float* __restrict__ g,
    const float* __restrict__ ln_w,
    const float* __restrict__ ln_b,
    const float* __restrict__ w_q,
    const float* __restrict__ w_k,
    const float* __restrict__ w_v,
    const float* __restrict__ w_g,
    const float* __restrict__ b_g,
    int B, int N, int S_in, int D_in, int H_in, int DH_in
) {
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    int s = blockIdx.x % S_in;
    int tmp = blockIdx.x / S_in;
    int n = tmp % N;
    int b = tmp / N;
    
    const float* x_ptr = x + ((b * N + n) * S_in + s) * D_in;
    
    __shared__ float x_shared[64];
    
    x_shared[tid * 2] = x_ptr[tid * 2];
    x_shared[tid * 2 + 1] = x_ptr[tid * 2 + 1];
    
    float sum = x_shared[tid * 2] + x_shared[tid * 2 + 1];
    for (int mask = 16; mask > 0; mask >>= 1) {
        sum += __shfl_xor_sync(0xFFFFFFFF, sum, mask);
    }
    float mean = sum / (float)D_in;
    
    float v0 = x_shared[tid * 2] - mean;
    float v1 = x_shared[tid * 2 + 1] - mean;
    x_shared[tid * 2] = v0;
    x_shared[tid * 2 + 1] = v1;
    
    float var_val = v0 * v0 + v1 * v1;
    for (int mask = 16; mask > 0; mask >>= 1) {
        var_val += __shfl_xor_sync(0xFFFFFFFF, var_val, mask);
    }
    float inv_std = rsqrtf(var_val / (float)D_in + 1e-5f);
    
    float n0 = v0 * inv_std * ln_w[tid * 2] + ln_b[tid * 2];
    float n1 = v1 * inv_std * ln_w[tid * 2 + 1] + ln_b[tid * 2 + 1];
    
    __syncthreads();
    x_shared[tid * 2] = n0;
    x_shared[tid * 2 + 1] = n1;
    __syncthreads();
    
    int feat = tid * 2;
    
    #pragma unroll
    for (int o = 0; o < 2; o++) {
        int f = feat + o;
        int row = f * D_in;
        float acc = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int j = 0; j < 64; j += 8) {
            acc += x_shared[j+0] * w_q[row + j+0];
            acc += x_shared[j+1] * w_q[row + j+1];
            acc += x_shared[j+2] * w_q[row + j+2];
            acc += x_shared[j+3] * w_q[row + j+3];
            acc += x_shared[j+4] * w_q[row + j+4];
            acc += x_shared[j+5] * w_q[row + j+5];
            acc += x_shared[j+6] * w_q[row + j+6];
            acc += x_shared[j+7] * w_q[row + j+7];
        }
        int h = f / DH_in;
        int d = f % DH_in;
        q[(((b * N + n) * H_in + h) * S_in + s) * DH_in + d] = acc;
    }
    
    #pragma unroll
    for (int o = 0; o < 2; o++) {
        int f = feat + o;
        int row = f * D_in;
        float acc = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int j = 0; j < 64; j += 8) {
            acc += x_shared[j+0] * w_k[row + j+0];
            acc += x_shared[j+1] * w_k[row + j+1];
            acc += x_shared[j+2] * w_k[row + j+2];
            acc += x_shared[j+3] * w_k[row + j+3];
            acc += x_shared[j+4] * w_k[row + j+4];
            acc += x_shared[j+5] * w_k[row + j+5];
            acc += x_shared[j+6] * w_k[row + j+6];
            acc += x_shared[j+7] * w_k[row + j+7];
        }
        int h = f / DH_in;
        int d = f % DH_in;
        k[(((b * N + n) * H_in + h) * S_in + s) * DH_in + d] = acc;
    }
    
    #pragma unroll
    for (int o = 0; o < 2; o++) {
        int f = feat + o;
        int row = f * D_in;
        float acc = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int j = 0; j < 64; j += 8) {
            acc += x_shared[j+0] * w_v[row + j+0];
            acc += x_shared[j+1] * w_v[row + j+1];
            acc += x_shared[j+2] * w_v[row + j+2];
            acc += x_shared[j+3] * w_v[row + j+3];
            acc += x_shared[j+4] * w_v[row + j+4];
            acc += x_shared[j+5] * w_v[row + j+5];
            acc += x_shared[j+6] * w_v[row + j+6];
            acc += x_shared[j+7] * w_v[row + j+7];
        }
        int h = f / DH_in;
        int d = f % DH_in;
        v[(((b * N + n) * H_in + h) * S_in + s) * DH_in + d] = acc;
    }
    
    #pragma unroll
    for (int o = 0; o < 2; o++) {
        int f = feat + o;
        int row = f * D_in;
        float acc = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int j = 0; j < 64; j += 8) {
            acc += x_shared[j+0] * w_g[row + j+0];
            acc += x_shared[j+1] * w_g[row + j+1];
            acc += x_shared[j+2] * w_g[row + j+2];
            acc += x_shared[j+3] * w_g[row + j+3];
            acc += x_shared[j+4] * w_g[row + j+4];
            acc += x_shared[j+5] * w_g[row + j+5];
            acc += x_shared[j+6] * w_g[row + j+6];
            acc += x_shared[j+7] * w_g[row + j+7];
        }
        acc += b_g[f];
        acc = 1.0f / (1.0f + expf(-acc));
        int h = f / DH_in;
        int d = f % DH_in;
        g[(((b * N + n) * H_in + h) * S_in + s) * DH_in + d] = acc;
    }
}

__global__ void msa_attn_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ q,
    const float* __restrict__ k,
    const float* __restrict__ v,
    const float* __restrict__ g,
    const float* __restrict__ mask,
    float* __restrict__ out,
    int B, int N, int S_in, int H_in, int DH_in
) {
    __shared__ float k_shared[32][16];
    __shared__ float v_shared[32][16];
    __shared__ float mask_shared[32];
    
    int b = blockIdx.x / (N * H_in);
    int tmp = blockIdx.x % (N * H_in);
    int n = tmp / H_in;
    int h = tmp % H_in;
    int s = threadIdx.x;
    
    if (s < S_in) mask_shared[s] = mask[((b * N + n) * S_in + s)];
    __syncwarp();
    
    int base = ((b * N + n) * H_in + h) * S_in * DH_in;
    
    float q_reg[16];
    float g_reg[16];
    
    #pragma unroll
    for (int d = 0; d < DH_in; d++) {
        q_reg[d] = q[base + s * DH_in + d];
        g_reg[d] = g[base + s * DH_in + d];
        k_shared[s][d] = k[base + s * DH_in + d];
        v_shared[s][d] = v[base + s * DH_in + d];
    }
    __syncwarp();
    
    float scale = rsqrtf((float)DH_in);
    float max_score = -1e20f;
    float scores[32];
    
    #pragma unroll
    for (int j = 0; j < S_in; j++) {
        float dot = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int d = 0; d < DH_in; d++) {
            dot += q_reg[d] * k_shared[j][d];
        }
        dot *= scale;
        if (mask_shared[j] == 0.0f) dot = -1e20f;
        scores[j] = dot;
        max_score = fmaxf(max_score, dot);
    }
    
    float sum_exp = 0.0f;
    #pragma unroll
    for (int j = 0; j < S_in; j++) {
        scores[j] = expf(scores[j] - max_score);
        sum_exp += scores[j];
    }
    float inv_sum = 1.0f / sum_exp;
    
    #pragma unroll
    for (int d = 0; d < DH_in; d++) {
        float val = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int j = 0; j < S_in; j++) {
            val += scores[j] * v_shared[j][d];
        }
        val *= inv_sum * g_reg[d];
        out[(((b * N + n) * S_in + s) * H_in + h) * DH_in + d] = val;
    }
}

__global__ void msa_out_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ attn_out,
    const float* __restrict__ w_out,
    const float* __restrict__ b_out,
    float* __restrict__ out,
    int B, int N, int S_in, int D_in, int H_in, int DH_in
) {
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    int s = blockIdx.x % S_in;
    int tmp = blockIdx.x / S_in;
    int n = tmp % N;
    int b = tmp / N;
    
    __shared__ float x_shared[64];
    
    int base = ((b * N + n) * S_in + s) * D_in;
    #pragma unroll
    for (int h = 0; h < H_in; h++) {
        #pragma unroll
        for (int d = 0; d < 8; d++) {
            int idx = h * 8 + d;
            x_shared[idx * 2] = attn_out[base + h * DH_in + d * 2];
            x_shared[idx * 2 + 1] = attn_out[base + h * DH_in + d * 2 + 1];
        }
    }
    __syncwarp();
    
    int feat = tid * 2;
    #pragma unroll
    for (int o = 0; o < 2; o++) {
        int f = feat + o;
        int row = f * D_in;
        float acc = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int j = 0; j < 64; j += 8) {
            acc += x_shared[j+0] * w_out[row + j+0];
            acc += x_shared[j+1] * w_out[row + j+1];
            acc += x_shared[j+2] * w_out[row + j+2];
            acc += x_shared[j+3] * w_out[row + j+3];
            acc += x_shared[j+4] * w_out[row + j+4];
            acc += x_shared[j+5] * w_out[row + j+5];
            acc += x_shared[j+6] * w_out[row + j+6];
            acc += x_shared[j+7] * w_out[row + j+7];
        }
        acc += b_out[f];
        out[(((b * S_in + s) * N + n) * D_in + f)] = acc;
    }
}

torch::Tensor msa_forward(
    torch::Tensor msa_repr,
    torch::Tensor msa_mask,
    torch::Tensor ln_w,
    torch::Tensor ln_b,
    torch::Tensor w_q,
    torch::Tensor w_k,
    torch::Tensor w_v,
    torch::Tensor w_g,
    torch::Tensor b_g,
    torch::Tensor w_out,
    torch::Tensor b_out
) {
    int B = msa_repr.size(0);
    int N = msa_repr.size(1);
    int S_val = msa_repr.size(2);
    int D_val = msa_repr.size(3);
    int H_val = D_val / 16;
    int DH_val = 16;
    
    auto q = torch::empty({B, N, H_val, S_val, DH_val}, msa_repr.options());
    auto k = torch::empty({B, N, H_val, S_val, DH_val}, msa_repr.options());
    auto v = torch::empty({B, N, H_val, S_val, DH_val}, msa_repr.options());
    auto g = torch::empty({B, N, H_val, S_val, DH_val}, msa_repr.options());
    auto attn_out = torch::empty({B, N, S_val, H_val, DH_val}, msa_repr.options());
    auto out = torch::empty({B, S_val, N, D_val}, msa_repr.options());
    
    dim3 grid1(B * N * S_val);
    dim3 block1(32);
    msa_proj_kernel<<<grid1, block1>>>(
        msa_repr.data_ptr<float>(),
        q.data_ptr<float>(), k.data_ptr<float>(), v.data_ptr<float>(), g.data_ptr<float>(),
        ln_w.data_ptr<float>(), ln_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        w_q.data_ptr<float>(), w_k.data_ptr<float>(), w_v.data_ptr<float>(), w_g.data_ptr<float>(), b_g.data_ptr<float>(),
        B, N, S_val, D_val, H_val, DH_val
    );
    
    dim3 grid2(B * N * H_val);
    dim3 block2(S_val);
    msa_attn_kernel<<<grid2, block2>>>(
        q.data_ptr<float>(), k.data_ptr<float>(), v.data_ptr<float>(), g.data_ptr<float>(),
        msa_mask.data_ptr<float>(),
        attn_out.data_ptr<float>(),
        B, N, S_val, H_val, DH_val
    );
    
    dim3 grid3(B * N * S_val);
    dim3 block3(32);
    msa_out_kernel<<<grid3, block3>>>(
        attn_out.data_ptr<float>(),
        w_out.data_ptr<float>(), b_out.data_ptr<float>(),
        out.data_ptr<float>(),
        B, N, S_val, D_val, H_val, DH_val
    );
    
    return out;
}
'''

class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, msa_dim, num_heads, dropout=0.0):
        super().__init__()
        self.num_heads = num_heads
        self.head_dim = msa_dim // num_heads
        assert msa_dim % num_heads == 0
        
        self.layer_norm = nn.LayerNorm(msa_dim)
        self.query = nn.Linear(msa_dim, msa_dim, bias=False)
        self.key = nn.Linear(msa_dim, msa_dim, bias=False)
        self.value = nn.Linear(msa_dim, msa_dim, bias=False)
        self.gate = nn.Linear(msa_dim, msa_dim)
        self.out_proj = nn.Linear(msa_dim, msa_dim)
        self.dropout = nn.Dropout(dropout)
        
        self.msa_forward_module = ext.load_inline(
            name="msa_attn_cuda_s1",
            cuda_sources=cuda_source,
            cpp_sources=cpp_source,
            functions=["msa_forward"],
            extra_cuda_cflags=["-O3", "--use_fast_math"],
            extra_ldflags=["-static-libstdc++"],
        )
    
    def forward(self, msa_repr, msa_mask):
        x = msa_repr.permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
        mask = msa_mask.permute(0, 2, 1).contiguous()
        
        return self.msa_forward_module.msa_forward(
            x, mask,
            self.layer_norm.weight, self.layer_norm.bias,
            self.query.weight, self.key.weight, self.value.weight,
            self.gate.weight, self.gate.bias,
            self.out_proj.weight, self.out_proj.bias
        )
